\subsubsection[{diopi\-Abs}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}D\-I\-O\-P\-I\-\_\-\-A\-P\-I diopi\-Error\-\_\-t diopi\-Abs (

\item[{diopi\-Tensor\-Handle\-\_\-t}]{out, }
\item[{diopi\-Const\-Tensor\-Handle\-\_\-t}]{input}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)}}\label{functions_8h_adc58e74772f3942e3d6da3856d8c52ab}


Computes the absolute value of each element in the input tensor element-\/wise. 


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{参数}
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em ctx} & Context environment. \\
\hline
 & {\em input} & Input tensor, type = \mbox{[}float16, float32, float64, int16, int32, int64, uint8, int8\mbox{]}. \\
\hline
\mbox{\tt out}  & {\em out} & the output tensor. type = \mbox{[}float16, float32, float64, int16, int32, int64, uint8, int8\mbox{]}. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\hypertarget{functions_8h_a34dbbde65e25c2904012b1bea1f0bed5}{\index{functions.\-h@{functions.\-h}!diopi\-Abs\-Inp@{diopi\-Abs\-Inp}}
\index{diopi\-Abs\-Inp@{diopi\-Abs\-Inp}!functions.h@{functions.\-h}}
\subsubsection[{diopi\-Abs\-Inp}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}D\-I\-O\-P\-I\-\_\-\-A\-P\-I diopi\-Error\-\_\-t diopi\-Abs\-Inp (

\item[{diopi\-Tensor\-Handle\-\_\-t}]{input}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)}}\label{functions_8h_a34dbbde65e25c2904012b1bea1f0bed5}


the in-\/place version of \hyperlink{functions_8h_adc58e74772f3942e3d6da3856d8c52ab}{diopi\-Abs()}. 


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{参数}
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em input} & the input and output tensor and will be stored result tensor. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\hypertarget{functions_8h_aa68add906b1e88b57ec5add3ad2ada4c}{\index{functions.\-h@{functions.\-h}!diopi\-Adam\-W@{diopi\-Adam\-W}}
\index{diopi\-Adam\-W@{diopi\-Adam\-W}!functions.h@{functions.\-h}}
\subsubsection[{diopi\-Adam\-W}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}D\-I\-O\-P\-I\-\_\-\-A\-P\-I diopi\-Error\-\_\-t diopi\-Adam\-W (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
\item[{diopi\-Context\-Handle\-\_\-t}]{ctx, }
\item[{diopi\-Tensor\-Handle\-\_\-t}]{input, }
\item[{diopi\-Tensor\-Handle\-\_\-t}]{grad, }
\item[{diopi\-Tensor\-Handle\-\_\-t}]{exp\-\_\-avg, }
\item[{diopi\-Tensor\-Handle\-\_\-t}]{exp\-\_\-avg\-\_\-sq, }
\item[{diopi\-Tensor\-Handle\-\_\-t}]{max\-\_\-exp\-\_\-avg\-\_\-sq, }
\item[{float}]{lr, }
\item[{float}]{beta1, }
\item[{float}]{beta2, }
\item[{float}]{eps, }
\item[{float}]{weight\-\_\-decay, }
\item[{int64\-\_\-t}]{step, }
\item[{bool}]{amsgrad}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)}}\label{functions_8h_aa68add906b1e88b57ec5add3ad2ada4c}


Implements Adam\-W optimizer. 


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{参数}
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em ctx} & Context environment. \\
\hline
 & {\em input} & the input tensor. type=\mbox{[}float16, float32, float64\mbox{]}. \\
\hline
 & {\em grad} & the grad tensor. type=\mbox{[}float16, float32, float64\mbox{]}. \\
\hline
 & {\em exp\-\_\-avg} & the first momentum is related to the number of iterations, that is, the gradient mean value of the i th iteration. type=\mbox{[}float16, float32, float64\mbox{]}. \\
\hline
 & {\em exp\-\_\-avg\-\_\-sq} & the second momentum is related to the number of iterations, that is, the mean value of the gradient square of the i iteration. type=\mbox{[}float16, float32, float64\mbox{]}. \\
\hline
 & {\em max\-\_\-exp\-\_\-avg\-\_\-sq} & the maximum second momentum. When the parameter 'amsgrad' is true, it will replace the second momentum to participate in the calculation. type=\mbox{[}float16, float32, float64\mbox{]}. \\
\hline
 & {\em lr} & learning rate. \\
\hline
 & {\em beta1} & coefficients used for computing running averages of gradient. \\
\hline
 & {\em beta2} & square of coefficients. \\
\hline
 & {\em eps} & term added to the denominator to improve numerical stability. \\
\hline
 & {\em weight\-\_\-decay} & weight decay coefficient. \\
\hline
 & {\em step} & step. \\
\hline
 & {\em amsgrad} & whether to use the A\-M\-S\-Grad variant of this algorithm from the paper {\ttfamily On the Convergence of Adam and Beyond}\-\_\-. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

Performs matrix multiplication between mat1 and mat2, multiplies the result by scalar value alpha, adds it to input tensor beta x input. 


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{参数}
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em ctx} & Context environment. \\
\hline
 & {\em input} & the input tensor. type = \mbox{[}float32, float64, float16\mbox{]}\mbox{]}. \\
\hline
 & {\em mat1} & the first martix. type = \mbox{[}float32, float64, float16\mbox{]}. \\
\hline
 & {\em mat2} & the second martix. type = \mbox{[}float32, float64, float16\mbox{]}. \\
\hline
 & {\em beta} & scale factor of input. type = \mbox{[}int32, int64, float32, float64\mbox{]}. \\
\hline
 & {\em alpha} & the scaling factor for the multiplication result of the tensors. type = \mbox{[}int32, int64, float32, float64\mbox{]}. \\
\hline
\mbox{\tt out}  & {\em out} & the output tensor. type = \mbox{[}float32, float64, float16\mbox{]}. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

Applies 2\-D average-\/pooling operation in k\-H×k\-W regions by step size s\-H×s\-W steps. 


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{参数}
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em ctx} & Context environment. \\
\hline
 & {\em input} & input tensor, type = \mbox{[}float32, float64\mbox{]} \\
\hline
 & {\em kernel\-\_\-size} & an array, the size of the pooling region. type = \mbox{[}int32, int64\mbox{]}. \\
\hline
 & {\em stride} & an array, the stride of the pooling operation. type = \mbox{[}int32, int64\mbox{]}. \\
\hline
 & {\em padding} & an array. type = \mbox{[}int32, int64\mbox{]}. \\
\hline
 & {\em ceil\-\_\-mode} & boolean, when set to True, uses ceil instead of floor in the formula to compute the output shape. type = \mbox{[}bool\mbox{]}. \\
\hline
 & {\em count\-\_\-include\-\_\-pad} & boolean, when True, zero-\/padding will be included in the mean calculation. type = \mbox{[}bool\mbox{]}. \\
\hline
 & {\em divisor\-\_\-override} & If specified, it will be used as the divisor when computing the average pooling, otherwise the default is to divide by the total number of pooling elements. \\
\hline
\mbox{\tt out}  & {\em out} & the output tensor. type = \mbox{[}float32, float64\mbox{]}. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

Measures thee Cross Entropy between the target and input probabilities. 


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{参数}
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em ctx} & Context environment. \\
\hline
 & {\em input} & Input tensor representing the unnormalized scores, often referred to as logits. type = \mbox{[}float32, float64\mbox{]}. \\
\hline
 & {\em target} & Target tensor representing the true class index or class probabilities. type = \mbox{[}float32, float64\mbox{]}. \\
\hline
 & {\em weight} & Manual rescaling weight for each class. type = \mbox{[}float32, float64\mbox{]}. \\
\hline
 & {\em reduction} & Specifies the reduction to apply to the output. \\
\hline
 & {\em ignore\-\_\-index} & Specifies a target value that is to be ignored and does not contribute to the input gradient. Only used when targets are class indices. type = \mbox{[}int32, int64\mbox{]}. \\
\hline
 & {\em label\-\_\-smoothing} & Float value in \mbox{[}0.\-0, 1.\-0\mbox{]}. Specifies the amount of smoothing to be applied while computing the loss. type = \mbox{[}float32, float64\mbox{]} \\
\hline
\mbox{\tt out}  & {\em out} & the output tensor. type = \mbox{[}float32, float64\mbox{]}. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{参数}

\hline
 & {\em input} & the input tensor, dividend. type = \mbox{[}float64, float32, float16, int64, int32, int16, int8, uint8, bool\mbox{]}. \\

\hline
 & {\em rounding\-\_\-mode} & Rounding mode applied to the result, None\-: no rounding is performed, if both input and other are integer types, the inputs are promoted to the default scalar type; trunc\-: truncate towards zero; floor\-: round down towards negative infinity for the result of the division. \\
\hline
\mbox{\tt out}  & {\em out} & the output tensor. type = \mbox{[}float64, float32, float16, int64, int32, int16, int8, uint8, bool\mbox{]}. \\

\hypertarget{functions_8h_ad5ba0b885b1e380c4638fcf694afa781}{\index{functions.\-h@{functions.\-h}!diopi\-Dropout@{diopi\-Dropout}}
\index{diopi\-Dropout@{diopi\-Dropout}!functions.h@{functions.\-h}}
\subsubsection[{diopi\-Dropout}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}D\-I\-O\-P\-I\-\_\-\-A\-P\-I diopi\-Error\-\_\-t diopi\-Dropout (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
\item[{diopi\-Context\-Handle\-\_\-t}]{ctx, }
\item[{diopi\-Tensor\-Handle\-\_\-t}]{out, }
\item[{diopi\-Tensor\-Handle\-\_\-t}]{mask, }
\item[{diopi\-Const\-Tensor\-Handle\-\_\-t}]{input, }
\item[{double}]{p, }
\item[{bool}]{train}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)}}\label{functions_8h_ad5ba0b885b1e380c4638fcf694afa781}


Randomly zeroes some of the elements of the input tensor with probability p using samples from a Bernoulli distribution. 


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{参数}
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em ctx} & Context environment. \\
\hline
 & {\em input} & the input tensor, type = \mbox{[}float32, float64\mbox{]}. \\
\hline
 & {\em p} & the probability of an element in the input tensor being zeroed out. type = \mbox{[}float32, float64\mbox{]}. \\
\hline
 & {\em train} & boolean, whether the module is in training mode. When set to False, the dropout operation will not be performed. type = \mbox{[}bool\mbox{]}. \\
\hline
\mbox{\tt out}  & {\em out} & the output tensor. type = \mbox{[}float32, float64\mbox{]}. \\
\hline
 & {\em mask} & A binary mask tensor of the same shape as the input tensor, where each element's value is either 0 or 1, indicating whether the corresponding neuron at that position is dropped or not. type = \mbox{[}int32\mbox{]}. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

)}}\label{functions_8h_ab154e410a30a50b72e1e2b6961f7ea1e}


It clips the tensor values within a range defined by the lower and upper bounds. Any values below the lower bound are set to the lower bound, and any values above the upper bound are set to the upper bound. 


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{参数}
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em ctx} & Context environment. \\
\hline
 & {\em input} & the input tensor,type = \mbox{[}float32, float64\mbox{]}. \\
\hline
 & {\em min\-\_\-val} & scalar, the lower bound. type = \mbox{[}float32, float64\mbox{]}. \\
\hline
 & {\em max\-\_\-val} & scalar, the upper bound. type = \mbox{[}float32, float64\mbox{]}. \\
\hline
\mbox{\tt out}  & {\em out} & the output tensor. type = \mbox{[}float32, float64\mbox{]}. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

\subsubsection[{diopi\-Max\-Pool2d}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}D\-I\-O\-P\-I\-\_\-\-A\-P\-I diopi\-Error\-\_\-t diopi\-Max\-Pool2d (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
\item[{diopi\-Context\-Handle\-\_\-t}]{ctx, }
\item[{diopi\-Tensor\-Handle\-\_\-t}]{out, }
\item[{diopi\-Const\-Tensor\-Handle\-\_\-t}]{input, }
\item[{{\bf diopi\-Size\-\_\-t}}]{kernel\-\_\-size, }
\item[{{\bf diopi\-Size\-\_\-t}}]{stride, }
\item[{{\bf diopi\-Size\-\_\-t}}]{padding, }
\item[{{\bf diopi\-Size\-\_\-t}}]{dilation, }
\item[{bool}]{ceil\-\_\-mode}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)}}\label{functions_8h_a3e22b0cc398fb0cbfe485bce29c46205}


Applies a 2\-D max pooling over an input signal composed of several input planes. 


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{参数}
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em ctx} & Context environment. \\
\hline
 & {\em input} & the input tensor. type = \mbox{[}float16, float32\mbox{]} \\
\hline
 & {\em kernel\-\_\-size} & an array, size of the pooling region. type = \mbox{[}int32, int64\mbox{]}. \\
\hline
 & {\em stride} & an array, stride of the pooling operation. type = \mbox{[}int32, int64\mbox{]}. \\
\hline
 & {\em padding} & an array, implicit negative infinity padding on both sides of the input tensor, its value should be $>$= 0 and $<$= kernel\-\_\-size / 2. type = \mbox{[}int32, int64\mbox{]}. \\
\hline
 & {\em dilation} & an array, spacing between the elements within the sliding window, its value should be greater than 0. type = \mbox{[}int32, int64\mbox{]}. \\
\hline
 & {\em ceil\-\_\-mode} & boolean, if True, use ceil instead of the default floor operation when computing the output shape. This ensures that every element in the input tensor is covered by a sliding window. type = \mbox{[}bool\mbox{]}. \\
\hline
\mbox{\tt out}  & {\em out} & the output tensor. type = \mbox{[}float16, float32\mbox{]}. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

Measures thee nll loss between the target and input probabilities. 


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{参数}
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em ctx} & Context environment. \\
\hline
 & {\em input} & Input tensor, usually representing log probabilities. type = \mbox{[}float32, float64\mbox{]} \\
\hline
 & {\em target} & Target tensor representing class indices, with values in the range of \mbox{[}0, C). type = \mbox{[}int64\mbox{]} \\
\hline
 & {\em weight} & weights manually assigned to each class. type = \mbox{[}float32, float64\mbox{]} \\
\hline
 & {\em reduction} & Loss reduction mode, which can be none, sum, or mean. \\
\hline
 & {\em ignore\-\_\-index} & Specifies a target value to be ignored and does not contribute to the input gradient. This parameter can only be used when the target contains class indices. type = \mbox{[}int32, int64\mbox{]}. \\
\hline
\mbox{\tt out}  & {\em out} & the output tensor. type = \mbox{[}float32, float64\mbox{]}. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

Sorts the elements of the input tensor along a given dimension in ascending order by value. 


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{参数}
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em ctx} & Context environment. \\
\hline
 & {\em input} & the intput tensor. type = \mbox{[}float16, float32, float64, int16, int32, int64, uint8, int8\mbox{]} \\
\hline
 & {\em dim} & the dimension to sort along. type = \mbox{[}int32, int64\mbox{]}. \\
\hline
 & {\em descending} & boolean, controls the sorting order (ascending or descending). \\
\hline
 & {\em stable} & a boolean pointer, selects a stable sorting algorithm to use, where stable sorting algorithms guarantee that the order of equal elements remains unchanged. \\
\hline
\mbox{\tt out}  & {\em values} & the sorted tensor. type = \mbox{[}float16, float32, float64, int16, int32, int64, uint8, int8\mbox{]}. \\
\hline
 & {\em indices} & the index of corresponding element in the sorted tensor. type = \mbox{[}int32, int64\mbox{]}. \\
\hline

\hline
 & {\em largest} & boolean, whether to return the top k largest elements. \\
\hline
 & {\em sorted} & boolean, whether to return the top k elements in sorted order. \\
\hline
\mbox{\tt out}  & {\em values} & the top-\/k value tensor. type = \mbox{[}float16, float32, float64, int16, int32, int64, uint8, int8\mbox{]}. \\
\hline
 & {\em indices} & the index of top-\/k value tensor. type = \mbox{[}int32, int64\mbox{]}. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

Returns a tensor that is a transposed version of input. The given dimensions dim0 and dim1 are swapped. 


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{参数}
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em ctx} & Context environment. \\
\hline
 & {\em input} & the input tensor. type = \mbox{[}float16, float32, float64, int16, int64, uint8, int8, bool, int32\mbox{]}. \\
\hline
 & {\em dim0} & The first dimension to be transposed. type = \mbox{[}int32, int64\mbox{]}. \\
\hline
 & {\em dim1} & The second dimension to be transposed. type = \mbox{[}int32, int64\mbox{]}. \\
\hline
\mbox{\tt out}  & {\em out} & the output tensor. type = \mbox{[}float16, float32, float64, int16, int64, uint8, int8, bool, int32\mbox{]}. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

Returns the unique elements of the input tensor. 


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{参数}
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em ctx} & Context environment. \\
\hline
 & {\em input} & the input tensor,type = \mbox{[}int64, float32, float64, float16, int16, int32, uint8, int8, bool\mbox{]} \\
\hline
 & {\em dim} & Specifies the dimension along which the duplicates are removed. It can be None, which means removing duplicates from the entire input tensor. \\
\hline
 & {\em sorted} & boolean, whether to sort the result in ascending order. \\
\hline
 & {\em return\-\_\-counts} & boolean, whether to return the count tensor \\
\hline
\mbox{\tt out}  & {\em out} & the output tensor. type = \mbox{[}int64, float32, float64, float16, int16, int32, uint8, int8, bool\mbox{]}. \\
\hline
 & {\em indices} & if none, return new indices of each element in the output tensor. type = \mbox{[}int32, int64\mbox{]}. \\
\hline
 & {\em counts} & representing the count of occurrences of each element in the output tensor. type = \mbox{[}int32, int64\mbox{]}. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

Return a tensor of elements selected from either x or y, depending on condition. 


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{参数}
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em ctx} & Context environment. \\
\hline
 & {\em condition} & A boolean tensor of the same shape as x and y. For elements/positions where the corresponding value is true, the value from x is returned, otherwise the value from y is returned. type = \mbox{[}uint8, bool\mbox{]}. \\
\hline
 & {\em input} & the input tensor. type = \mbox{[}float16, float32, float64, int16, int32, int64, uint8, int8, bool\mbox{]} \\
\hline
 & {\em other} & the other tensor. type = \mbox{[}float16, float32, float64, int16, int32, int64, uint8, int8, bool\mbox{]} \\
\hline
\mbox{\tt out}  & {\em out} & the output tensor. type = \mbox{[}float16, float32, float64, int16,int32, int64, uint8, int8, bool\mbox{]}. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
